                Illustrations of arrangements for purposes of section 20(2A)</b></label></p><p class="HeadingParagraph filter"><span class="whitespace">&nbsp;</span><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="item" value="Sc10-" id="chk1e9e8f01-00e0-4c26-89f5-353ae8e95d1f" /> <label for="chk1e9e8f01-00e0-4c26-89f5-353ae8e95d1f"><b>TENTH  SCHEDULE
                Prescribed information</b></label></p><p class="HeadingParagraph filter"><span class="whitespace">&nbsp;</span><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="item" value="xv-" id="chkfb321d18-0aca-4518-aad0-0617b9bf53c1" /> <label for="chkfb321d18-0aca-4518-aad0-0617b9bf53c1"><b>Legislative History</b></label></p><p class="HeadingParagraph filter"><span class="whitespace">&nbsp;</span><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="item" value="xv-ta-oc2-" id="chkLEGISLATION_ABBREVIATIONS" /> <label for="chkLEGISLATION_ABBREVIATIONS"><b>Abbreviations</b></label></p><p class="HeadingParagraph filter"><span class="whitespace">&nbsp;</span><input class="form-check-input" type="checkbox" name="item" value="xy-" id="chkaa8f1e86-f020-475a-bab2-87cf0da4939c" /> <label for="chkaa8f1e86-f020-475a-bab2-87cf0da4939c"><b>Comparative Table</b></label></p></div>

                    <div id="legisContent">
                        <table width="100%"><tr><td class="part"  id="P13-"><div class="partNo">PART 3</div><table width="100%"><tr><td class="partHdr" id="P13-he-">IMPOSITION AND EXTENT OF TAX</td></tr></table><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr7-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Goods and services tax</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>7.</strong>&#xA0;&#xA0;A tax to be known as Goods and Services Tax is charged in accordance with the provisions of this Act on the supply of goods and services (including anything treated as such a supply) and on the importation of goods.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr8-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Scope of tax</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>8.</strong><a name="pr8-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;Tax is charged on any supply of goods or services made in Singapore where it is a taxable supply made by a taxable person in the course or furtherance of any business carried on by the taxable person.</span><a name="pr8-ps1A-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(1A)&#xA0;&#xA0;Without affecting subsection&#160;(1), tax is charged on any Seventh Schedule supply where it is a taxable supply made by a taxable person in the course or furtherance of any business carried on by the taxable person.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr8-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;A person is a taxable person for the purposes of this Act while the person is or is required to be registered under this Act.</td></tr></table><a name="pr8-ps2A-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2A)&#xA0;&#xA0;A taxable supply is&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for subsection&#160;(1), a supply of goods or services made in Singapore other than an exempt supply; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">for subsection (1A), a Seventh Schedule supply.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr8-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;Tax on any supply of goods or services is a liability of the person making the supply and (subject to provisions on accounting and payment) becomes due at the time of supply.</td></tr></table><a name="pr8-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;Tax is charged, levied and payable on any importation of goods (other than an exempt import) as if it were customs duty or excise duty and as if all goods imported into Singapore are dutiable and liable to customs duty or excise duty.<div class="amendNote">[19/2012]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr9-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Registration</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>9.</strong><a name="pr9-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;The First Schedule has effect in relation to the registration of taxable persons.</span><a name="pr9-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;The Minister may by order amend the First&#160;Schedule.</td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr10-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Meaning of &#8220;supply&#8221;</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>10.</strong><a name="pr10-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;The Second Schedule applies for determining what is, or is treated as, a supply of goods or a supply of services.</span><a name="pr10-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to any provision made by the Second&#160;Schedule and to orders made under subsection&#160;(3)&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">&#8220;supply&#8221; in this Act includes all forms of supply and reverse charge supplies, but not anything done otherwise than for a consideration;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">anything which is not a supply of goods but is done for a consideration (including, if so done, the granting, assignment or surrender of any right) is a supply of services.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr10-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;The Minister may by order amend the Second&#160;Schedule and may also provide by order with respect to any description of transaction&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">that it is treated as a supply of goods and not as a supply of services;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">that it is treated as a supply of services and not as a supply of goods; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">that it is treated as neither a supply of goods nor a supply of services.</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr10-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;Without affecting subsection&#160;(3), an order made under that subsection may provide that paragraph&#160;5(3) of the Second&#160;Schedule is not to apply, in relation to goods of any prescribed description used or made available for use in prescribed circumstances, so as to make that a supply of services under that paragraph.</td></tr></table><a name="pr10-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of this section, where goods are manufactured or produced from any other goods, those other goods are treated as incorporated in the firstmentioned goods.</td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr10A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Making of supply: bare trustees</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>10A.</strong>&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of this Act, any supply made by a bare trustee relating to any goods, intellectual property rights or licence to use any intellectual property rights held by the bare trustee, is treated as a supply made by the persons or person for whose business the bare trustee holds the goods, rights or licence.<div class="amendNote">[31/2014]</div></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Time of supply: general provisions</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11.</strong><a name="pr11-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;This section and sections&#160;11A, 11B, 11C, 12 and 12A apply for determining the time when a supply of goods or services is treated as taking place for the purposes of this Act.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 52/2018]</div></span><a name="pr11-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;A supply of goods or services (other than a reverse charge supply) is treated for the purposes of this Act as taking place at the time when&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person making the supply issues an invoice or receives any consideration in respect of it; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where both events occur, the first of the 2 events occurs,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply is covered by the invoice or consideration.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 52/2018]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;Despite subsection&#160;(2), where a supply is&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a supply of goods consisting of the grant, assignment or surrender of any interest in or right over land (other than the grant of a tenancy or lease where the whole or part of the consideration for that grant is payable periodically and attributed to separate periods of the term of the tenancy or lease);</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a supply of goods or services made by a person who applies to the Comptroller for this subsection to apply in determining when the person’s supplies of goods or services take place, and the Comptroller allows the person’s application; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a supply of goods made by an agent that is treated under section&#160;33(2) as a supply by the agent as principal,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">then, unless subsection&#160;(4) applies, the supply is treated for the purposes of this Act as taking place as follows:</td></tr></table><table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case of a supply of goods&#160;&#8212;<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr11-ps3-p1d-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">if the goods are to be removed, at the time of the removal; and</td></tr><tr id="pr11-ps3-p1d-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">if the goods are not to be removed, at the time when they are made available to the person to whom they are supplied; and</td></tr></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case of a supply of services, at the time when the services are performed,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply is covered by the goods that are removed or made available, or the services that are performed, as the case may be.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 24/2011]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;If, before the time under subsection&#160;(3), the person making a supply referred to in that subsection issues an invoice or receives any consideration in respect of it, the supply is treated as taking place at the time when&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the invoice is issued or the consideration is received; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where both events occur, the first of the 2 events occurs,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply is covered by the invoice or consideration.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 24/2011]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purpose of determining the time when a supply of goods or services (other than a reverse charge supply) is treated as taking place for the purposes of this Act, where a person provides a document to himself, herself or itself which purports to be an invoice in respect of a supply of goods or services to him, her or it by another person, the Comptroller may treat that invoice as an invoice issued by the other person as the supplier.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 52/2018]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Time of supply: exceptions to section&#160;11(2) and (3)</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11A.</strong><a name="pr11A-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;Section&#160;11(2) and (3) does not apply where any subsection herein applies, except to the extent specified in that subsection.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></span><a name="pr11A-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of paragraphs&#160;1(1) and (2), 1A(1) and (2) and 2 (in relation to sub‑paragraph&#160;(2)(<em>a</em>)(i) of that paragraph) of the First&#160;Schedule, the supply is treated as taking place at the time when&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person making the supply issues an invoice or receives any consideration in respect of it; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where both events occur, the first of the 2 events occurs,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply is covered by the invoice or consideration.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 52/2018]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11A-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of regulations made under section&#160;19(13)(<em>b</em>) and (<i>c</i>) in respect of tax on a supply of goods or services made to a taxable person that the taxable person may count as the taxable person’s input tax, the supply is treated as taking place at the time when&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the taxable person making the supply issues an invoice or receives any consideration in respect of it; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where both events occur, the first of the 2 events occurs,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply is covered by the invoice or consideration.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11A-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;Where there is a supply of goods by virtue only of a transfer or disposal of assets under paragraph&#160;5(1) of the Second&#160;Schedule, the supply is treated as taking place&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the goods are transferred or disposed of as specified in that paragraph&#160;for no consideration, when the goods are transferred or disposed of as specified in that paragraph; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the goods are transferred or disposed of as specified in that paragraph&#160;for a consideration, in accordance with section&#160;11(2) or (3), as the case may be.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr11A-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&#xA0;&#xA0;Where there is a supply of services by virtue only of paragraph&#160;5(3) of the Second&#160;Schedule, the supply is treated as taking place&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the goods are appropriated to the use mentioned in that paragraph&#160;for no consideration, on the last day of the supplier’s prescribed accounting period, or of each such accounting period, in which the goods are used or made available for the use; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where the goods are appropriated to the use mentioned in that paragraph&#160;for a consideration, in accordance with section&#160;11(2) or (3), as the case may be.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr11A-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&#xA0;&#xA0;If goods (being sent or taken on approval or sale or return or similar terms) are removed before it is known whether a supply will take place, a supply of the goods is treated as taking place 12&#160;months after the removal; except that where the person from whom the goods are removed issues an invoice or receives any consideration in respect of those goods before the expiry of the 12‑month period, a supply of the goods is treated as taking place at the time when&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the invoice is issued or the consideration is received; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where both events occur, the first of the 2 events occurs.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11B-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Time of supply: exceptions to section&#160;11(2)</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11B.</strong><a name="pr11B-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;Section&#160;11(2) does not apply to the extent any subsection herein applies.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></span><a name="pr11B-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#160;(7), where a person who is, or is required to be, registered under this Act makes a supply of goods or services to another person who is not entitled under sections&#160;19 and 20 to credit for the whole or any part of the tax on the supply, and&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">but for this subsection, the supply would under section&#160;11(2) be treated as taking place after the date on which the person is, or is required to be, registered under this Act; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">prior to that date&#160;&#8212;<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr11B-ps2-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">in the case of a supply of goods&#160;&#8212;<table class="p3_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr11B-ps2-p1b-p2i-p3A-"><td class="p3No">(A)</td><td class="p3Txt">if the goods are to be removed, they had been removed; or</td></tr><tr id="pr11B-ps2-p1b-p2i-p3B-"><td class="p3No">(B)</td><td class="p3Txt">if the goods are not to be removed, they had been made available to the other person; or</td></tr></table></td></tr><tr id="pr11B-ps2-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">in the case of a supply of services, the services had been performed,</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">then the person making the supply must, if the other person so requests, treat the supply as taking place when the goods were removed or made available, or the services were performed (as the case may be), and the supply is so treated for the purposes of this Act.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11B-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#160;(7) and section&#160;11C(4), where a person who makes a supply of goods or services is connected within the meaning of paragraph&#160;3 of the Third&#160;Schedule with the person to whom the supply is made, and&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case of a supply of goods&#160;&#8212;<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr11B-ps3-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">if the goods are to be removed, they are removed; or</td></tr><tr id="pr11B-ps3-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">if the goods are not to be removed, they are made available to the person to whom they are supplied; or</td></tr></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">in the case of a supply of services, the services are performed,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">then the supply is treated as taking place at the end of 12&#160;months after the goods have been removed or made available, or the services have been performed (as the case may be), to the extent that it is not covered by any invoice already issued or consideration already received.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 52/2018]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11B-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;The Minister may by regulations prescribe supplies of goods or services which are excluded from subsection&#160;(3).<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11B-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to subsections&#160;(3) and (7), where&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a person making a supply of goods or services also makes a supply of financial services referred to in paragraph&#160;1 of Part&#160;1 of the Fourth Schedule to the recipient of the goods or services in respect of the supply of the goods or services; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the financial services provide for payment by instalments,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">then the supply of the goods or services is treated as wholly taking place at the time when&#160;&#8212;</td></tr></table><table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the invoice in respect of the first instalment is issued or the first instalment is paid; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where both events occur, the first of the 2 events occurs.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 19/2012]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr11B-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to subsection&#160;(7), where, pursuant to a supply of goods or services&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a taxable person&#160;&#8212;<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr11B-ps6-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">in the case of a supply of goods&#160;&#8212;<table class="p3_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr11B-ps6-p1a-p2i-p3A-"><td class="p3No">(A)</td><td class="p3Txt">if the goods are to be removed, allows their removal; or</td></tr><tr id="pr11B-ps6-p1a-p2i-p3B-"><td class="p3No">(B)</td><td class="p3Txt">if the goods are not to be removed, makes them available to the person to whom they are supplied; or</td></tr></table></td></tr><tr id="pr11B-ps6-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">in the case of a supply of services, performs the services,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="p1SO"  style="font-size:13pt">as the case may be, whether on a single occasion or on different occasions;</td></tr></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the taxable person then ceases to be a taxable person; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">no invoice or consideration covering the whole of the supply has been issued or received (as the case may be) by the taxable person prior to the date when the person ceases to be a taxable person,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">the supply of goods or services is treated as taking place on the day immediately before the day the person ceases to be a taxable person, to the extent that it is not covered by any invoice already issued or consideration already received.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11B-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subsections&#160;(2), (3), (5) and (6) do not apply in relation to&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any supply of goods referred to in section&#160;11(3)(<em>a</em>) or (<i>c</i>); or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any supply of goods or services made by a person whose application has been allowed by the Comptroller under section&#160;11(3)(<em>b</em>).<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr11C-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Time of supply: reverse charge supplies</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>11C.</strong><a name="pr11C-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;This section applies to determine when a reverse charge supply of a recipient mentioned in section&#160;14 takes place for the purposes of this Act (including for the purposes of paragraph&#160;1B of the First Schedule).<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div></span><a name="pr11C-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to subsections (2A), (3), (3A), (4), (6) and (7), the reverse charge supply takes place when&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the person or branch that in fact supplies the distantly taxable goods or services to the recipient issues an invoice, or the recipient pays any consideration for those distantly taxable goods or services; or</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">where both events occur, the first of the 2 events occurs,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply of distantly taxable goods or services is covered by the invoice or consideration.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11C-ps2A-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2A)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to subsection (3A), where —<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a supply of distantly taxable goods or services that is made to a recipient gives rise to a reverse charge supply;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the recipient pays an amount to the supplier (whether directly or indirectly) as tax on the supply of goods or services in fact made to the recipient purportedly under section&#160;8(1A) (whether or not the supply was in fact chargeable to tax under section&#160;8(1A)); and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supplier reimburses the recipient (whether directly or indirectly) for that amount,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">then the recipient may treat the reverse charge supply as taking place at the earlier of&#160;&#8212;</td></tr></table><table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the date on which a revised invoice in respect of the supply in fact made is issued by the supplier; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the date on which the recipient receives the reimbursement of that amount,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply is covered by the revised invoice, or by consideration paid for that supply, as reduced by the reimbursement.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[Act 35 of 2022 wef 01/01/2023]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11C-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subject to subsection (3A), where the recipient is registered under this Act, the recipient may, for any period during which the recipient receives distantly taxable goods or services that are the subject of the recipient’s reverse charge supplies, treat each of those reverse charge supplies as taking place at the earlier of&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the date on which the supply in fact made to the recipient and giving rise to that reverse charge supply is entered into the books of account or other records of the recipient; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the date on which the recipient pays any consideration for that supply,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply of distantly taxable goods or services is covered by the entry or consideration.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11C-ps3A-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3A)&#xA0;&#xA0;If the recipient applies subsection (3) to its reverse charge supplies, the recipient may, for a reverse charge supply in the circumstances described in subsection (2A)(<em>a</em>), (<em>b</em>) and (<i>c</i>), treat the reverse charge supply instead as taking place at the earlier of&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the date on which the supply for which reimbursement of the amount was received is entered into amount,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">to the extent that the supply is covered by the entry or consideration paid for that supply as reduced by already paid.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 35 of 2022 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11C-ps5-"></a><table class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11C-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">then the recipient may treat the reverse charge supply as taking place when the distantly taxable goods were delivered (to the extent of the delivery) or the to the extent that it is not covered by any invoice already issued or consideration already paid.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11C-ps8-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(8)&#xA0;&#xA0;Despite subsections (2), (2A), (3), (3A), (4), (6) and (7), where&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1" in the form and manner, and within the time, required by the Comptroller.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr11C-ps10-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td which the recipient is regarded as having paid the consideration for the purposes of this section is the later date.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Time of supply: directions and regulations</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>12.</strong><a name="pr12-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;Despite sections&#160;11, 11A, 11B and 11C, the Comptroller may, at the request of a taxable person, by direction in writing alter the time at which supplies made or received by the taxable person (or such supplies made or received by the taxable person as may be specified in the direction) are treated as taking place, either&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td id="pr12-ps1-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">at times or on dates determined by or by reference to the occurrence of some event described in the direction; or</td></tr><tr or</td></tr></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">by directing that those supplies (to the extent that they are not treated as taking place at the time any invoice is issued or any consideration is received or paid in respect thereof) be treated as taking place&#160;&#8212;<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr12-ps1-p1b-p2i-"><td id="pr12-ps1-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">at the end of the relevant working period (as so defined).<div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 52/2018]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></span><a name="pr12-ps1A-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(1A)&#xA0;&#xA0;Despite sections 11, 11A and 11B, the Comptroller may, at the request of a registered (Seventh Schedule — pay only) person, by direction in writing alter the time at which any specified supply made by the person (whether or not a Seventh Schedule supply) is to be treated as taking place, by directing that that supply be treated as taking place at the time or on the date determined by or by reference to the occurrence of some event described in the direction, whether the resulting time or date is earlier or later than the time or date that would otherwise apply.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a person.</td></tr></table><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr12-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;Despite sections&#160;11, 11A, 11B and 11C, the Minister may by regulations&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">make provision with respect to the time at which (despite sections&#160;11, 11A, 11B, 11C and 38(4)) a supply is treated as taking place in cases where&#160;&#8212;<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr12-ps2-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">it is a supply of goods or services for a consideration the whole or part of which is determined or payable periodically, or from time to time, or at the end of any period;</td></tr><tr id="pr12-ps2-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">it class="pTxt">prescribe when consideration for a supply of goods or services of a specified type, or provided in a specified manner, is to be regarded as having been received or paid.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010; 37/2017; 52/2018]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr12-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;Regulations made under subsection&#160;(2)(<em>a</em>) may provide for goods or services to be treated as separately and successively supplied at prescribed times or intervals.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr12A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Time deducted.<div class="amendNote">[33/2019]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps3B-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3B)&#xA0;&#xA0;Where the reverse charge supply of a recipient arises from&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a supply of services mentioned in section&#160;14(1)(<em>b</em>)(ii); or<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">a supply of services mentioned in section&#160;30(1A),</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1N2SO"  style="font-size:13pt">then, for the purpose of determining the value of the reverse charge supply, any of the following that is included as part of the consideration for the services in fact supplied may be deducted:</td></tr></table><table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any salary or wages relating to the employees of (as the case may be) the branch or member of the group outside Singapore making the supply of services;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">interest;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any proportionate amount of mark-up in respect of such salary or wages and interest in paragraphs&#160;(<em>c</em>) and (<i>d</i>), respectively.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018; 33/2019]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps3C-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3C)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of the application of the Third Schedule, where the reverse charge supply arises from a supply of distantly taxable goods mentioned in section 14(1)(<em>a</em>)(ii) or a supply of services mentioned in section 14(1)(<em>b</em>)(ii), the branches mentioned in section 14(1)(<em>a</em>)(ii) or (<em>b</em>)(ii) (as the case may be) are treated as persons connected with each other.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps3D-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3D)&#xA0;&#xA0;A Seventh Schedule supply of goods treated as made by a redeliverer has a value that is equal to the consideration paid for the goods by the customer.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;Where a supply of any goods or services (including a supply mentioned in subsection (2A)(<em>a</em>) or (<i>b</i>)) is not the only matter to which a consideration in money relates, the supply is deemed to be for such part of the consideration as is properly attributable to it.<div class="amendNote">[52/2018]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps4A-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4A)&#xA0;&#xA0;Where a person makes a supply of related services to a customer of a Seventh Schedule supply of goods in relation to that supply of goods, the consideration for the related services is to be included as part of the consideration for the Seventh Schedule supply of goods if&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the consideration for the supply of the related services is determined by reference to those goods;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services is made, arranged or assisted by the supplier or underlying supplier of those goods;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services is directly in connection with those goods;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services would be zero-rated under section 21 in the absence of this subsection; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services and those goods do not form a single supply.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 35 of 2022 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps4B-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4B)&#xA0;&#xA0;Subsection (4A) does not apply to a redeliverer that is treated as making a supply of goods under the Seventh Schedule.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps4C-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4C)&#xA0;&#xA0;Where a reverse charge supply arises from a supply of distantly taxable goods mentioned in section 14(1)(<em>a</em>) and the recipient also receives a supply of related services, the consideration for the related services is to be included as part of the consideration for the supply of the distantly taxable goods if&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the consideration for the supply of the related services is determined by reference to those goods;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services is made, arranged or assisted by the supplier of those goods;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services is directly in connection with those goods;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>d</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services would, if the supply of the services were made by a taxable person in Singapore, be a supply of international services which is zero-rated under section 21 in the absence of this subsection; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>e</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">the supply of the related services and those goods do not form a single supply.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of this Act, the open market value of a supply of goods or services is taken to be the amount that would fall to be taken as its value under subsection&#160;(2) if the supply were for such consideration in money as would be payable by a person who has no relationship with any person which would affect that consideration.</td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&#xA0;&#xA0;The Minister may by order amend the Third&#160;Schedule and provide for the determination of the value of a supply of goods or services otherwise than in accordance with this section.</td></tr></table><a name="pr17-ps7-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(7)&#xA0;&#xA0;In this section&#160;&#8212;<table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“redeliverer” and “underlying supplier” have the meanings given by paragraph 1(1) of the Seventh Schedule;</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="def"  style="font-size:13pt">“related services”, in relation to a Seventh Schedule supply of goods or a supply of distantly taxable goods that gives rise to a reverse charge supply, means the services supplied by any person (whether or not the supplier or underlying supplier of the goods) for the purposes of&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">processing and preparing the goods for transportation and delivery; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1DefNo">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pDefTxt">delivering the goods, or arranging or assisting in the delivery of the goods, including insurance and transportation.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div><div class="amendNote">[Act 35 of 2022 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr18-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Value of imported goods</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>18.</strong><a name="pr18-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of this Act, the value of imported goods is determined as follows:<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">subject to paragraph&#160;(<em>b</em>), the value of the goods is the aggregate of the following:<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1a-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">the value of the goods determined in accordance with such method of valuation as may be prescribed pursuant to section&#160;22 of the Customs Act&#160;1960; and</td></tr><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1a-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">so far as not already included in the value referred to in sub‑paragraph&#160;(i), all taxes, duties and other charges levied either outside or, by reason of importation, within Singapore (except goods and services tax);</td></tr></table></td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">subject to the Third&#160;Schedule, where goods from outside Singapore enter Singapore under customs control and one or more supplies of those goods involve&#160;&#8212;<table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1b-p2i-"><td class="p2No">(i)</td><td class="p2Txt">the goods being removed from a place under such customs control; or</td></tr><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1b-p2ii-"><td class="p2No">(ii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the goods being made available while under such customs control,</td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="p1SO"  style="font-size:13pt">the value of the goods is the aggregate of the following:</td></tr></table><table class="p2_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1b-p2iii-"><td class="p2No">(iii)</td><td class="p2Txt">the value of the last of such supplies; and</td></tr><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1b-p2iv-"><td class="p2No">(iv)</td><td class="p2Txt">so far as not already included in the value referred to in sub-paragraph&#160;(iii)&#160;&#8212;<table class="p3_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1b-p2iv-p3A-"><td class="p3No">(A)</td><td class="p3Txt">all taxes, duties and other charges levied either outside or, by reason of importation, within Singapore (except goods and services tax); and</td></tr><tr id="pr18-ps1-p1b-p2iv-p3B-"><td class="p3No">(B)</td><td class="p3Txt">all costs by way of commission, packing, transport and insurance and all other costs, charges and expenses incidental to the sale and the delivery of the goods up to the port or place of importation.<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></span><a name="pr18-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;In the application of the Customs Act&#160;1960, by virtue of section&#160;26, to any goods which are not subject to either customs duty or excise duty, such goods are construed as being under &#8220;customs control&#8221; within the meaning of section&#160;3(2) of the Customs Act&#160;1960&#160;&#8212;<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">as if they are dutiable goods; and</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">as if the reference to a licensed warehouse in section&#160;3(2) of the Customs Act&#160;1960 includes a warehouse or other place licensed under section&#160;37(5)(<em>b</em>).<div class="amendNote">[20/2010]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div><div class="prov1"><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Hdr" id="pr18A-"><span class="noBold"></span><span class="">Entry value of items of goods</span></td></tr></table><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov1Txt"><strong>18A.</strong><a name="pr18A-ps1-"></a><span class="prov2TxtIL">&#8212;(1)&#xA0;&#xA0;This section applies for the purpose of determining the entry value of any item of goods.</span><a name="pr18A-ps2-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(2)&#xA0;&#xA0;Except for the purposes of determining whether the supply of any item of goods gives rise to a reverse charge supply under section 14, the entry value of the item is the consideration for the supply of the item, less all of the following amounts that are included in that consideration:<table class="p1_1"  style="font-size:13pt" width="100%"><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>a</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">transport and insurance charges for the item for the period beginning when the item leaves the country or territory from which it is supplied and ending when it is delivered to a place in the customs territory;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>b</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any tax chargeable on the supply of the item under section 8;</td></tr><tr><td class="p1No">(<em>c</em>)</td><td class="pTxt">any customs duty or excise duty.</td></tr></table></td></tr></table><a name="pr18A-ps3-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(3)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of subsection (2), the supplier of the goods may use a reasonable estimate of any of the amounts mentioned in subsection (2)(<em>a</em>), (<em>b</em>) and (<i>c</i>), based on the information available to the supplier at the point of sale of the goods.</td></tr></table><a name="pr18A-ps4-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(4)&#xA0;&#xA0;Instead of applying subsections (2) and (3), the supplier may elect for the entry value of any item of goods to be the value determined in accordance with section 18 for the item.</td></tr></table><a name="pr18A-ps5-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(5)&#xA0;&#xA0;An election made under subsection (4) must be made by notifying the Comptroller in such form and manner and within such time as the Comptroller may require.</td></tr></table><a name="pr18A-ps6-"></a><table width="100%"><tr><td class="prov2Txt">(6)&#xA0;&#xA0;For the purposes of determining whether the supply of any item of goods gives rise to a reverse charge supply under section&#160;14, the entry value of the item is the value determined in accordance with section 18 for the item.<div class="amendNote">[Act 34 of 2021 wef 01/01/2022]</div></td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div></td></tr></table>
                    </div>
